  <COMMENT line1="4" col1="1" line2="4" col2="29" start="649" end="677">#' kallisto wrapper functions</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="5" col1="1" line2="5" col2="2" start="811" end="812">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="6" col1="1" line2="6" col2="74" start="973" end="1046">#' Run the abundance quantification tool \code{kallisto} on a set of FASTQ</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="7" col1="1" line2="7" col2="80" start="1135" end="1214">#' files. Requires \code{kallisto} (\url{http://pachterlab.github.io/kallisto/})</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="8" col1="1" line2="8" col2="78" start="1297" end="1374">#' to be installed and a kallisto feature index must have been generated prior</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="9" col1="1" line2="9" col2="78" start="1459" end="1536">#' to using this function. See the kallisto website for installation and basic</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="10" col1="1" line2="10" col2="22" start="1621" end="1642">#' usage instructions.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="11" col1="1" line2="11" col2="2" start="1783" end="1784">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="12" col1="1" line2="12" col2="79" start="1945" end="2023">#' @param targets_file character string giving the path to a tab-delimited text</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="13" col1="1" line2="13" col2="80" start="2107" end="2186">#' file with either 2 columns (single-end reads) or 3 columns (paired-end reads)</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="14" col1="1" line2="14" col2="80" start="2269" end="2348">#' that gives the sample names (first column) and FastQ file names (column 2 and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="15" col1="1" line2="15" col2="79" start="2431" end="2509">#' if applicable 3). The file is assumed to have column headers, although these</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="16" col1="1" line2="16" col2="16" start="2593" end="2608">#' are not used.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="17" col1="1" line2="17" col2="75" start="2755" end="2829">#' @param transcript_index character string giving the path to the kallisto</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="18" col1="1" line2="18" col2="61" start="2917" end="2977">#' index to be used for the feature abundance quantification.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="19" col1="1" line2="19" col2="77" start="3079" end="3155">#' @param single_end logical, are single-end reads used, or paired-end reads?</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="20" col1="1" line2="20" col2="80" start="3241" end="3320">#' @param output_prefix character string giving the prefix for the output folder</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="21" col1="1" line2="21" col2="77" start="3403" end="3479">#' that will contain the kallisto results. The default is \code{"output"} and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="22" col1="1" line2="22" col2="80" start="3565" end="3644">#' the sample name (column 1 of \code{targets_file}) is appended (preceded by an</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="23" col1="1" line2="23" col2="15" start="3727" end="3741">#' underscore).</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="24" col1="1" line2="24" col2="72" start="3889" end="3960">#' @param fragment_length scalar integer or numeric giving the estimated</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="25" col1="1" line2="25" col2="82" start="4051" end="4132">#' average fragment length. Required argument if \code{single_end} is \code{TRUE},</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="26" col1="1" line2="26" col2="77" start="4213" end="4289">#' optional if \code{FALSE} (kallisto default for paired-end data is that the</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="27" col1="1" line2="27" col2="43" start="4375" end="4417">#' value is estimated from the input data).</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="28" col1="1" line2="28" col2="74" start="4537" end="4610">#' @param fragment_standard_deviation scalar numeric giving the estimated </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="29" col1="1" line2="29" col2="68" start="4699" end="4766">#' standard deviation of read fragment length. Required argument if </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="30" col1="1" line2="30" col2="80" start="4861" end="4940">#' \code{single_end} is \code{TRUE}, optional if \code{FALSE} (kallisto default </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="31" col1="1" line2="31" col2="75" start="5023" end="5097">#' for paired-end data is that the value is estimated from the input data).</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="32" col1="1" line2="32" col2="79" start="5185" end="5263">#' @param n_cores integer giving the number of cores (nodes/threads) to use for</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="33" col1="1" line2="33" col2="78" start="5347" end="5424">#' the kallisto jobs. The package \code{parallel} is used. Default is 2 cores.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="34" col1="1" line2="34" col2="76" start="5509" end="5584">#' @param n_bootstrap_samples integer giving the number of bootstrap samples</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="35" col1="1" line2="35" col2="79" start="5671" end="5749">#' that kallisto should use (default is 0). With bootstrap samples, uncertainty</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="36" col1="1" line2="36" col2="34" start="5833" end="5866">#' in abundance can be quantified.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="37" col1="1" line2="37" col2="77" start="5995" end="6071">#' @param bootstrap_seed scalar integer or numeric giving the seed to use for</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="38" col1="1" line2="38" col2="78" start="6157" end="6234">#' the bootstrap sampling (default used by kallisto is 42). Optional argument.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="39" col1="1" line2="39" col2="77" start="6319" end="6395">#' @param correct_bias logical, should kallisto's option to model and correct</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="40" col1="1" line2="40" col2="77" start="6481" end="6557">#' abundances for sequence specific bias? Requires kallisto version 0.42.2 or</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="41" col1="1" line2="41" col2="10" start="6643" end="6652">#' higher.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="42" col1="1" line2="42" col2="74" start="6805" end="6878">#' @param plaintext logical, if \code{TRUE} then bootstrapping results are</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="43" col1="1" line2="43" col2="52" start="6967" end="7018">#' returned in a plain text file rather than an HDF5</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="44" col1="1" line2="44" col2="45" start="7129" end="7173">#' \url{https://www.hdfgroup.org/HDF5/} file.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="45" col1="1" line2="45" col2="73" start="7291" end="7363">#' @param kallisto_version character string indicating whether or not the</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="46" col1="1" line2="46" col2="77" start="7453" end="7529">#' version of kallisto to be used is \code{"pre-0.42.2"} or \code{"current"}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="47" col1="1" line2="47" col2="75" start="7615" end="7689">#' This is required because the kallisto developers changed the output file</COMMENT>
